
-----title
婺源 (出生地)

href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1153&endYear=1160')">1153-1160年</a>　居乡求学。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年</a>　丁父忧。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1163')">1162-1163年</a>　居家丁父忧。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1167')">1164-1167年</a>　居乡求学。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年</a>　夏，识友人齐彦邦，彦邦预言其明年必登第。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年</a>　秋登名于乡书。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='b157e23c94e54b17bc16ff41a418a3cf_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b157e23c94e54b17bc16ff41a418a3cf");'><span id='b157e23c94e54b17bc16ff41a418a3cf_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1174')">1170-1174年</a>，33-37岁</div><div id='b157e23c94e54b17bc16ff41a418a3cf' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年</a>　春，齐彦邦来访，王炎写序相送。作品：《送齐彦邦序》<div id='poem_1279784' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1279784' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1279784?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送齐彦邦序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1170年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30187, "南宋", "王炎", "poem_title_1279784")'>王炎</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1279784_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1279784'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1279784'>以五行之休王、五纬之伏逆进退而决人之得丧寿夭穷通，以卜筮而占事之休咎，二术难乎精者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1279784_comment'></div>而同邑人齐君彦邦实兼之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1279784_comment'></div>其胸中所得极有根源，扣之衮衮不竭，如江流于峡，河析于龙门三经之险，悬流下走而东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1279784_comment'></div>其抵掌议论，旋转而掉厉，如掷丸于阪，走珠于盘，鸷鸟高翔于千仞之上而迫于疾风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1279784_comment'></div>其愈试而愈中，中而愈奇，又如巧有力者开数石之弦，注镞于百步之外而饮羽于的也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1279784_comment'></div>戊子夏始识诸城之东，彦邦谓予曰：「吾详考于术，执事今年秋登名于乡书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1279784_comment'></div>明年春中太常第无疑也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1279784_comment'></div>予笑曰：「子言过矣，幸无以我为戏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1279784_comment'></div>不然，岂轻有所许以求容者乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1279784_comment'></div>彦邦不平曰：「借术贾佞者吾羞焉，何待我薄也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1279784_comment'></div>吾据术以自献其情，纵不信，庸何伤」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1279784_comment'></div>予因以失辞为谢，心实未之然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1279784_comment'></div>既而皆如其言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1279784_comment'></div>庚寅春，来过敝庐，谈笑道旧，而不以既中之言自矜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1279784_comment'></div>予于是始知其心，盖向之自负其术以介，而今之不矜似义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1279784_comment'></div>得其术，未得其为人，则知彦邦之浅者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1279784_comment'></div>彦邦不幸丧明，且不乐苟合，闻其言者多不悦，故余详论其术与其为人以饯其行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1279784_comment'></div>苟有问焉者，勿苦其言之不甘，庶几可以尽其所怀云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1279784_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年</a>　冬，韩毅伯道婺源，来访于云溪。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年</a>　是年有诗。作品：《山间偶成二绝》<div id='poem_72104' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_72104' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/72104?labeling=true' target='_blank'>山间偶成二绝<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（庚寅）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30187, "南宋", "王炎", "poem_title_72104")'>王炎</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_72104_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_72104'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_72104'>人家鸡犬近相闻，村落纡回古木深。<div id='poem_sentence_0_72104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_72104'>山客一来尘想尽，水声终日奏鸣琴。<div id='poem_sentence_1_72104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_72104'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_72104_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_72103' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_72103' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/72103?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（庚寅）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_72103_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_72103'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_72103'>隔枝啼鸟唤幽梦，排闼青山无世情。<div id='poem_sentence_0_72103_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_72103'>绿树阴阴遮日影，虚窗卧看白云行。<div id='poem_sentence_1_72103_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_72103'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_72103_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年</a>　居家。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1172')">1172年</a>　丁母忧，友人韩毅伯走数百里来唁。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1172')">1172年</a>　是年有诗。作品：《游砚山》<div id='poem_72841' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_72841' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/72841?labeling=true' target='_blank'>游砚山</a><span class='authorDate'>（壬辰）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_72841'>产璞芙蓉坑，金声而玉德。<div id='poem_sentence_1_72841_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_72841'>冈峦外<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_72841", 72841, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>钩联</span>，地势中断隔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_72841_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_72841'>曲坞八九家，路入羊豕迹。<div id='poem_sentence_3_72841_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_72841'>涧水抱石根，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_72841", 72841, "Clauses/9/Comments/1")'>石骨</span><span class='inlineComment2'>（王本作髓）</span>多绀碧。<div id='poem_sentence_4_72841_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_72841'>北山上搀天，南山势蟠伏。<div id='poem_sentence_5_72841_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_72841'>砚工二<span class='inlineComment2'>（王本作一）</span>百指，日凿崔嵬腹。<div id='poem_sentence_6_72841_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_72841'>篝灯砺斧斤，深入逾百尺。<div id='poem_sentence_7_72841_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_72841'>我行冒风雨，周览不知夕。<div id='poem_sentence_8_72841_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_72841'>夜宿茅茨下，青灯照岑寂。<div id='poem_sentence_9_72841_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_72841'>酒阑呼匠氏，访之语纤悉。<div id='poem_sentence_10_72841_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_72841'>冰蚕吐银丝，鲛人织雾縠。<div id='poem_sentence_11_72841_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_72841'>巧手琢磨之，价直黄<span class='inlineComment2'>（王本作千）</span>金镒。<div id='poem_sentence_12_72841_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_72841'>断岩半倾攲，旧穴久湮塞。<div id='poem_sentence_13_72841_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_72841'>旁求得他材，饮水不受墨。<div id='poem_sentence_14_72841_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_72841'>坚滑已支庶<span class='inlineComment2'>（王本作靡）</span>，粗燥乃臧获。<div id='poem_sentence_15_72841_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_72841'>信知天壤间，尤物神所惜。<div id='poem_sentence_16_72841_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_72841'>罕见固为贵，有亦未易识。<div id='poem_sentence_17_72841_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_72841'>珉玉混一区，语尽三叹息。<div id='poem_sentence_18_72841_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_72841'>摩挲<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>苍藓崖，此言可镌刻。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1174')">1173-1174年</a>　居家丁母忧。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='78f41165396f43cfb2a5b0d9d8ff2239_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("78f41165396f43cfb2a5b0d9d8ff2239");'><span id='78f41165396f43cfb2a5b0d9d8ff2239_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1186&endYear=1186')">1186年</a>，49岁</div><div id='78f41165396f43cfb2a5b0d9d8ff2239' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1186&endYear=1186')">1186年</a>　居乡。作品：《念奴娇（海棠时过江潭）》<div id='poem_72931' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_72931' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/72931?labeling=true' target='_blank'>念奴娇 海棠时过江潭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1185年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30187, "南宋", "王炎", "poem_title_72931")'>王炎</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_72931_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_72931'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_72931'>晓来雨过，遍海棠枝上，胭脂如滴。<div id='poem_sentence_0_72931_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_72931'>桃杏不堪来比并，信是倾城倾国。<div id='poem_sentence_1_72931_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_72931'>藏韵收香，谁能描貌，阁尽诗人笔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_72931_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_72931'>从教睡去，为留银烛终夕。<div id='poem_sentence_3_72931_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_72931'>不待过了清明，绿阴结子，无处寻春色。<div id='poem_sentence_4_72931_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_72931'>簌簌轻红飞一片，便觉临风悽恻。<div id='poem_sentence_5_72931_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_72931'>莫道无情，嫣然一笑，也似曾相识。<div id='poem_sentence_6_72931_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_72931'>惜花无主，自怜身是行客。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_72931_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='9319a53f036e4fe7ad369299857007c1_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("9319a53f036e4fe7ad369299857007c1");'><span id='9319a53f036e4fe7ad369299857007c1_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1201&endYear=1202')">1201-1202年</a>，64-65岁</div><div id='9319a53f036e4fe7ad369299857007c1' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1201&endYear=1201')">1201年2月</a>　二月，放罢，主管武夷山冲佑观，寓居婺源清化。作品：《程允夫集序》<div id='poem_1279808' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1279808' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1279808?labeling=true' target='_blank'>程允夫集序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1201年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30187, "南宋", "王炎", "poem_title_1279808")'>王炎</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1279808_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1279808'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1279808'>予与程君允夫居同邑、学同术，允夫在辈流中藉藉有声，而予出处差池，未之识也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1279808_comment'></div>及随牒宦游，始邂逅于庐陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1279808_comment'></div>见其说经史、论古今，亹亹令人属耳不厌，于是始恨相识之晚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1279808_comment'></div>允夫亦为予倾倒底里，过于旧交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1279808_comment'></div>予自清江秩满，入中都为博士，久不闻问，因询乡人之来者，则允夫已捐馆舍矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1279808_comment'></div>又四年，予始来归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1279808_comment'></div>其婿黄君昭远集允夫所著诗文属序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1279808_comment'></div>予读之终编，大抵理胜而词彩附之，淘鍊檃括，俱不苟作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1279808_comment'></div>盖允夫早名荐书，晚缀仕籍，素所蕴蓄不获见于事业，而惟寓于其文，故所成就如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1279808_comment'></div>此足为不朽，计于地下无憾矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1279808_comment'></div>昔者先友竹溪居士张公公予尝为予言：「为文犹之善酿，稻秫必时，曲糵必齐，水泉必香。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1279808_comment'></div>投于一器，既熟，去其糟粕，沈浊在下，菁华在上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1279808_comment'></div>其色澄清，其气芬郁，其味醇旨，此良酝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1279808_comment'></div>惟文亦然」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1279808_comment'></div>读允夫之文者，当以是观之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1279808_comment'></div>著作郎、军器少监奉祠双溪王炎序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1279808_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1202&endYear=1202')">1202年</a>　寓居婺源清化，有诗纪事。作品：《即事（久辍囊中句）》《壬戌立春日（寓清化）》《贺吴兴郡王生日（壬戌）》<div id='poem_72412' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_72412' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/72412?labeling=true' target='_blank'>即事<span class='inlineComment2'>（时寓清化）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1202年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30187, "南宋", "王炎", "poem_title_72412")'>王炎</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_72412_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_72412'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_72412'>久辍囊中句，时看肘后方。<div id='poem_sentence_0_72412_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_72412'>有家如旅舍，无事似僧房。<div id='poem_sentence_1_72412_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_72916_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_72916'>销凝。<div id='poem_sentence_4_72916_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_72916'>衣故几时更。<div id='poem_sentence_5_72916_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_72916'>又谁复卿卿。<div id='poem_sentence_6_72916_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_72916'>念镜里琴中，离鸾有恨，别鹄无情。<div id='poem_sentence_7_72916_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_72916'>齐眉处同笑语，但有时、梦见似平生。<div id='poem_sentence_8_72916_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_72916'>愁对婵娟三五，素光暂缺还盈。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_72916_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='00e33f12d4a4406aa268693ab453f59c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("00e33f12d4a4406aa268693ab453f59c");'><span id='00e33f12d4a4406aa268693ab453f59c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1209&endYear=1218')">1209-1218年</a>，72-81岁</div><div id='00e33f12d4a4406aa268693ab453f59c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1209&endYear=1209')">1209年</a>　是秋，子恕辞官陪伴其归返故园。作品：《旧苦左臂痛今春自霅川罢官寓居会稽秋中闻德莹弟讣音幽忧无聊背胁得疾痛楚殆不可忍早夜思家恕子慨然投劾同归壮年游宦计日月为考舍之而去可谓爱亲矣予年过七十兄弟凋落人生非金石谁能长存有子而孝使予返故园父子相依钟鸣漏尽终于牖下可以含笑入地成唐律一篇以著其意》（萧萧华发更何为）<div id='poem_72548' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_72548' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/72548?labeling=true' target='_blank'>病中恕子投劾同归<span class='inlineComment2'>（题原缺，据王本补）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1209年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30187, "南宋", "王炎", "poem_title_72548")'>王炎</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_72548_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_72548'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_72548'>萧萧华发更何为，元是穷乡一布衣。<div id='poem_sentence_0_72548_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_72548'>同产弟兄谁见在，馀生父子独相依。<div id='poem_sentence_1_72548_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_72548'>我缘多病念家切，汝为爱亲投劾归。<div id='poem_sentence_2_72548_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_72548'>出处不齐难逆定，时来还自刺天飞。<div id='poem_sentence_3_72548_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_72548'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_72548_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1210&endYear=1210')">1210年</a>　闲居双溪。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1211&endYear=1211')">1211年</a>　闲居双溪，中秋有词。作品：《浪淘沙（辛未中秋与文蔚达可饮）》<div id='poem_72946' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_72946' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/72946?labeling=true' target='_blank'>浪淘沙令 辛未中秋与文蔚达可饮</a><span class='authorDate'>（1211年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30187, "南宋", "王炎", "poem_title_72946")'>王炎</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_72946_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_72946'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_72946'>月色十分圆。<div id='poem_sentence_0_72946_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_72946'>风露娟娟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_72946_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_72946'>木犀香里凭栏干。<div id='poem_sentence_2_72946_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_72946'>河汉横斜天似水，玉鉴光寒。<div id='poem_sentence_3_72946_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_72946'>草草具杯盘。<div id='poem_sentence_4_72946_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_72946'>相对苍颜。<div id='poem_sentence_5_72946_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_72946'>素娥莫惜少留连。<div id='poem_sentence_6_72946_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_72946'>秋气平分蟾兔满，动是经年。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_72946_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1211&endYear=1211')">1211年</a>　是年修“双溪之园”，自作记。作品：《双溪园记》<div id='poem_1279835' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1279835' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1279835?labeling=true' target='_blank'>双溪园记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1211年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30187, "南宋", "王炎", "poem_title_1279835")'>王炎</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1279835_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1279835'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1279835'>婺源县治东十有五里，双溪汇为一潭，潭西北樊之以蓺竹木，王氏叟晦叔游衍之地也，题其门曰「双溪之园」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1279835_comment'></div>入门有屋，前轩而后俯，松露滴沥，竹风萧爽，杖履徜徉，可以自适其适，命曰「识分之堂」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1279835_comment'></div>堂之左有庵，修广十有二肘，覆以棕榈，山行罢，于此少休，命曰「息肩之庵」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1279835_comment'></div>庵左败屋数椽，撤而新之，中设一榻，几有《周易》一卷，壁间挂一白拂、一古琴，燕坐无事，时玩三圣微言，倦则曲肱而卧，命曰「巢安之寮」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1279835_comment'></div>堂之背负山为亭，前种杂花数种，花开时白酒一杯，悠然自酌，山鸟啸歌，为我所喜，心境和畅，无忧可消，命曰「留春」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1279835_comment'></div>自此循麓委折而上，至山椒，双溪交流，千山竞秀，使人目不得瞬，命曰「画笥」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1279835_comment'></div>北行高岗，至绝顶，四顾豁然，命曰「一览」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1279835_comment'></div>下有松坡，有茗坞，有莲塘，可着亭榭三四，俸馀已竭，未能鸠工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1279835_comment'></div>画笥南下俯寒潭，听鸣濑夜静，上下空阔，与月相宜，于是筑玩月之台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1279835_comment'></div>台之下以其隙地莳杂药，种桑苧，于是结灌畦之庐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1279835_comment'></div>庐之外筱荡蔚然，潭水如玻瓈盆，限以樵牧之径，乃跨径为桥入竹间，竹水生风，可以却暑，于是置枕流之石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1279835_comment'></div>双溪之境大略如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1279835_comment'></div>客或曰：「公摘《池上》篇中语名堂若庵、若寮，意欲自拟于白傅乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1279835_comment'></div>彼为近臣，为宫师，公不如其达也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1279835_comment'></div>东皋所入，一岁千斛，公不如其富也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1279835_comment'></div>取进士、贤良两科以才称，为天子谏官以直闻，篇章脍炙，传诵于幽闺妇女、草野儿童之口而外达夷裔，公不如其名垂世、文行远也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1279835_comment'></div>甲第在觚棱侧，池台之胜闻于京师，公于荒山野水间有园数亩，不如其居之丽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1279835_comment'></div>樊素、小蛮能歌善舞，饮酣乐作，继以霓裳之奏，公虽黄头之奴、赤脚之婢且无之，歌舞管弦复何如其处之乐也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1279835_comment'></div>引以自比，将为人嗤」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1279835_comment'></div>晦叔曰：「吾视白公不如者六，而胜之者三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1279835_comment'></div>白公生以龟□自随，没以侄孙为嗣，吾有子有孙，时温凊，奉烝尝，视彼孰俞」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1279835_comment'></div>曰：「胜之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1279835_comment'></div>「白公栖心禅梵，自谓安闲，暮年得风缓之疾，遣蛮、素二姬，意复悽怆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1279835_comment'></div>吾虽多病，行步未伛偻，耳目未昏瞆，视彼孰俞」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1279835_comment'></div>曰：「胜之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1279835_comment'></div>「白公七十有六而终，吾今七十有四，若窒嗜欲以养精，息思虑以养神，薄滋味以养气，体未遽溘先朝露，视我孰愈」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1279835_comment'></div>曰：「胜之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1279835_comment'></div>「然则，有无相方，无愧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1279835_comment'></div>穷达贫富得丧毁誉皆身外事，何较为」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1279835_comment'></div>客退，因识其说，又系之曰：吾歙中一布衣书生耳，携书一束，干进有司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1279835_comment'></div>既仕，不敢一日舍书不观，学虽不及古人，文虽不过今人，前辈颇相许可，得于人者多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1279835_comment'></div>少时家立四壁，宦游四十馀年，有田以食，有宅以居，得于上者多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1279835_comment'></div>同登第者十不一存，同改秩者五不一存，同升两学、游三馆者亦多入鬼录，吾幸无恙，得于天者多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1279835_comment'></div>上焉不能自拔于俗以为高，下焉不能自媚于世以为容，既老，退为清时幸民，一丘一壑，专而有之，他尚何求？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1279835_comment'></div>夫壮则宜出，老则宜退处，理然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1279835_comment'></div>出不劳无以立事，处不逸无以存身，亦理然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1279835_comment'></div>吾将返锁门关，不与物接，以养颓龄，挟争气、好臧否者不可入吾门，尚势利、计有无者不可登吾堂，好声名、矜才智者不可入吾庵，论文字、谈世事者不可入吾寮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1279835_comment'></div>有踰此言，山灵将以俗诮，溪神将为愚羞，戒之哉！</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_37_1279835'></div><div id='poem_sentence_37_1279835_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1212&endYear=1212')">1212年</a>　闲居双溪，有诗述怀。作品：《密室（壬申冬）》《舟行到满塘（壬申）》《壬申十二月二十八夜雷》<div id='poem_72825' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_72825' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/72825?labeling=true' target='_blank'>密室<span id='poem_content_72825'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_72825'>密室可附火，小窗聊借明。<div id='poem_sentence_0_72825_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_72825'>风寒皆不到，温饱更何营。<div id='poem_sentence_1_72825_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_72825'>省事事自少，养心心亦清。<div id='poem_sentence_4_72825'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_72825_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_72712' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_72712' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_72712'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_72712'>蘋花双港静，莲叶一舟轻。<div id='poem_sentence_0_72712_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_72712'>白石波间走，青山路外行。<div id='poem_sentence_1_72712_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_72712'>鯈鱼方自乐，鸥鸟不须惊。<div id='poem_sentence_2_72712_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_72712'>拥鼻蓬窗底，翛然午吹生。<div id='poem_sentence_3_72712_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_72712'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_72712_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_72348' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_72348' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/72348?labeling=true' target='_blank'>壬申<span class='inlineComment2'>（王本作嘉定壬申）</span>十二月二十八夜雷</a><span class='authorDate'>（1212年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_title_72348_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_72348'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_72348'>残腊方淫雨，中宵忽怒雷。<div id='poem_sentence_0_72348_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_72348'>更长频展转，梦断但惊猜。<div id='poem_sentence_1_72348_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_72348'>冻雪何时解，春风几日来。<div id='poem_sentence_2_72348_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_72348'>龙蛇今在蛰，墐户不宜开。<div id='poem_sentence_3_72348_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_72348'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_72348_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1212&endYear=1212')">1212年</a>　闲居双溪，有词述怀。作品：《清平乐（壬申除夜）》<div id='poem_72951' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_72951' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/72951?labeling=true' target='_blank'>清平乐 嘉定壬申除夜</a><span class='authorDate'>（1212年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30187, "南宋", "王炎", "poem_title_72951")'>王炎</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_72951_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_72951'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_72951'>一杯椒醑。<div id='poem_sentence_0_72951_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_72951'>惜饮难成醉。<div id='poem_sentence_1_72951_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_72951'>爆竹声中人未睡。<div id='poem_sentence_2_72951_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_72951'>共道今宵守岁。<div id='poem_sentence_3_72951_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_72951'>不如且就衾裯。<div id='poem_sentence_4_72951_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_72951'>谁能细数更筹。<div id='poem_sentence_5_72951_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_72951'>三百六旬过了，明朝却是年头。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_72951_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1213&endYear=1213')">1213年</a>　闲居双溪，清明日有诗抒怀。作品：《清明日先茔挂楮钱（癸酉）》<div id='poem_72557' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_72557' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/72557?labeling=true' target='_blank'>清明日先茔挂楮钱</a><span class='authorDate'>（癸酉）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30187, "南宋", "王炎", "poem_title_72557")'>王炎</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_72557_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_72557'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_72557'>昔人最重去坟墓，绝喜归来老一丘。<div id='poem_sentence_0_72557_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_72557'>岂是他山无笋蕨，只缘故国有松楸。<div id='poem_sentence_1_72557_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_72557'>百年暂住人间世，千古俱为地下游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1279474_comment'></div>圣心兼爱，遂推赐帛之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1279474_comment'></div>拜手知荣，扪躬增感<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1279474_comment'></div>恭惟陛下内行禹俭，外广尧仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1279474_comment'></div>方遵周礼之始裘，岁云秋矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1279474_comment'></div>因念豳诗之无褐，寒者衣之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1279474_comment'></div>乃班在笥之华，遍逮充廷之士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1279474_comment'></div>虽存旧典，实出洪私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1279474_comment'></div>严凝变而春温，被服资于天覆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_72614_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_72614'>不应令节亦虚度，特为萸菊觞新醪。<div id='poem_sentence_3_72614_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' -----title
当涂

class='poemContent' id='poem_content_72629'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_72629'>丁男负荷力已疲，弱妻稚子颜色悲。<div id='poem_sentence_0_72629_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_72629'>亲戚坟墓谁忍弃，嗟尔岂愿为流移。<div id='poem_sentence_1_72629_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_72629'>春蚕成茧谷成穗，输入豪家无孑遗。<div id='poem_sentence_4_72629'>但忧衔恨委沟壑，岂暇怀土安室庐。<div id='poem_sentence_4_72629_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_72629'>故乡既已不可居，他乡为客将谁依。<div id='poem_sentence_5_72629_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_72629'>黄鸡啄黍白酒熟，去家未久吾怀归。<div id='poem_sentence_6_72629_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_72629'>农桑不事得温饱，见尔令人颜忸怩。<div id='poem_sentence_7_72629_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_72629'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_72629_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
崇阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='42396a55d39a46e986690d3c3788ca73_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("42396a55d39a46e986690d3c3788ca73");'><span id='42396a55d39a46e986690d3c3788ca73_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1178')">1175-1178年</a>，38-41岁</div><div id='42396a55d39a46e986690d3c3788ca73' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年</a>　调鄂州崇阳簿。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1178')">1176-1178年</a>　在崇阳簿任上。作品：《喜雨赋并序》《喜雨歌》《见林鄂州（子中）》<div id='poem_1279425' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1279425' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1279425?labeling=true' target='_blank'>喜雨赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1176年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30187, "南宋", "王炎", "poem_title_1279425")'>王炎</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1279425_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1279425'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1279425'>丙申夏四月，武昌阖郡不雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1279425_comment'></div>越五月三日，崇阳宰吴侯以诚祷，雨获优渥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1279425_comment'></div>按《春秋》僖公三年春正月不雨，夏四月不雨，六月雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1279425_comment'></div>说者曰：「书不雨者，闵雨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1279425_comment'></div>书雨者，喜雨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1279425_comment'></div>喜雨者有意于民也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1279425_comment'></div>今吴侯祷雨以诚，不崇朝而雨随之，可谓有志于民矣，作《喜雨赋》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1279425_comment'></div>其词曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1279425'>岁行于涒滩之辰，斗建于实沈之次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1279425_comment'></div>环鄂渚之七县，值亢阳之为沴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1279425_comment'></div>风自南而且霾，日将北而如燬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1279425_comment'></div>云霓郁而不兴，旱魃骄而孰御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1279425_comment'></div>策余马于郊牧，喧龙骨之咿嚘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1279425_comment'></div>滮池潴其既竭，陂堰支其断流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1279425_comment'></div>视衍沃而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1279425", 1279425, "Clauses/31/Comments/0")'>龟坼</span>，况高田之未耰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1279425_comment'></div>苗已悴而半槁，惧西畴之不收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1279425_comment'></div>几张颐而待哺，举蹙頞而增忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1279425_comment'></div>粤桃溪之令君，念民命之惟谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1279425_comment'></div>兹土旷而农惰，虽儋石而无蓄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1279425_comment'></div>繄告籴之少艰，米翔踊而如玉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1279425_comment'></div>傥既月而旱甚，民必仆于沟渎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1279425_comment'></div>讲雩祀之故事，虚心斋而竭诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1279425_comment'></div>谒梵王之莲宫，羞蘋蘩之洁清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1279425_comment'></div>欸仙伯之灵岩，释舆马而草行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1279425_comment'></div>阴曀曀以随盖，飔悠悠而拥旌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1279425_comment'></div>柱础湿其有汗，钟鼓鞳而无声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1279425_comment'></div>纷举手以加额，曰雨兆其已形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1279425_comment'></div>龟日蒇仪，肃我庭宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1279425_comment'></div>驾龙骖螭，攸届攸止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1279425_comment'></div>云将前驱，雨师踵至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1279425_comment'></div>越三日而为霖，罄一同而均利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1279425_comment'></div>稼芃芃而骤苏，浍汩汩而如注。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1279425_comment'></div>免为殍于凶年，占筑场于乐岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1279425_comment'></div>沸舆颂而载涂，歌令君之阴赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1279425_comment'></div>其歌曰：「霢霂兮涵濡，污邪兮满车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1279425_comment'></div>其饟兮有黍，稻粳兮可炊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1279425_comment'></div>岂弟之泽，民肥不臞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1279425_comment'></div>我字我抚，公留勿归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1279425_comment'></div>均此大惠，公归勿徐」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1279425_comment'></div>吴侯闻而哂之曰：「父老之言何美之溢也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1279425_comment'></div>向也民忧而忧，此吏责也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1279425_comment'></div>今也民喜而喜，吏不敢以为德也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1279425_comment'></div>然旱而祷，祷而雨，如重负之获释也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1279425_comment'></div>酌我醑醴，旅我殽核，合僚友而一笑，吾敢忘夫帝力」！</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1279425_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_72836' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_72836' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/72836?labeling=true' -----title
咸安
-----detail

class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年</a>，41岁</div><div id='72db66406e644d11a997ba756394a84e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年</a>　在崇阳任上，公干到咸宁，有诗纪之。作品：《题咸宁江宰德先清远堂》<div id='poem_72861' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_72861' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/72861?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题咸宁江宰德先清远堂</a><span class='authorDate'>（1178年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_72861'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_72861'>筑屋俯平湖，百顷风漪涟。<div id='poem_sentence_0_72861_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_72861'>湖底行白云，湖外横青山。<div id='poem_sentence_1_72861_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_72861'>仙官踏两凫，游戏来人间。<div id='poem_sentence_2_72861_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_72861'>清都在天上，欲去懒著鞭。<div id='poem_sentence_3_72861_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='inlineComment2'>（王本作螯）</span>手，为民奏鸣弦。<div id='poem_sentence_5_72861_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_72861'>潘郎儿辈尔，栽花作春妍。<div id='poem_sentence_6_72861_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_72861'>渊明未甚高，料理种秫田。<div id='poem_sentence_7_72861_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_72861'>捲箔坐绳床，香吐一缕烟。<div id='poem_sentence_8_72861_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_72861'>白鸟入空濛，飞鸿度云边。<div id='poem_sentence_9_72861_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_72861'>个里不著愁，心与物共閒。<div id='poem_sentence_10_72861_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_72861'>渔榔劝客饮，玉色亦粲然。<div id='poem_sentence_11_72861_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_72861'>目极意不尽，老蟾生莫天。<div id='poem_sentence_12_72861_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_72861'></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_72861_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
长沙
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='34e1c72b0b8f415fa6481d5aee286a1e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("34e1c72b0b8f415fa6481d5aee286a1e");'><span id='34e1c72b0b8f415fa6481d5aee286a1e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1182&endYear=1185')">1182-1185年</a>，45-48岁</div><div id='34e1c72b0b8f415fa6481d5aee286a1e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1182&endYear=1182')">1182年</a>　为潭州教授，受到知潭州、湖南安抚使李椿器重。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1182&endYear=1182')">1182年</a>　是年孟冬，为外家祠堂作记。作品：《汪端公濆祠堂记》<div id='poem_1279831' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1279831' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1279831?labeling=true' target='_blank'>汪端公祠堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1182年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30187, "南宋", "王炎", "poem_title_1279831")'>王炎</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1279831_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1279831'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1279831'>婺源东九十里曰鳙溪，居人惟汪氏一族，其始祖曰端公，以官称也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1279831_comment'></div>唐大中间，汪氏自歙徙而来此，至今十传矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1279831_comment'></div>李氏时盗贼蜂起，端公以勇略选为三梧将，捍御乡闾，拒贼死之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1279831_comment'></div>众慕其义，遂立庙镇旁，而鳙溪咸恩僧舍亦有祠象在焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1279831_comment'></div>乡人奉事甚严，春秋祭祀以时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1279831_comment'></div>岁久，庙坏碑仆，十世孙叔谋曰：「庙祠不存，则无以揭虔妥灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1279831_comment'></div>然立庙重事，祠宇弊，曷新之」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1279831_comment'></div>于是富者出财，壮者效力，既讫工，来请记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1279831_comment'></div>炎窃惟汪氏得姓自鲁颍州侯始，童子汪踦能执干戈以卫社稷，夫子正色称之，汪氏之名遂号经史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1279831_comment'></div>及隋末，越国公奄据歙、宣、杭、睦、婺、饶，六州之民庙事之，荐以阴功，进爵为王，而汪氏由是滋大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1279831_comment'></div>惟端公之□，其忠义似童子，其智略似越公，惜其地偏位下，不克焜耀于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1279831_comment'></div>然则，生而有劳，殁而有灵，庙食不绝，亦可谓豪杰之士矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1279831_comment'></div>故我先提刑云溪翁及通判何公侃俱记其灵异之迹，传信不诬，则端公位虽不登祀典，奉以祠庙宜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1279831_comment'></div>公讳濆，春秋三十二岁，阶至银青光禄大夫，勋至上柱国，官至检校太子宾客兼御史大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1279831_comment'></div>一子四孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1279831_comment'></div>举族二千馀指，馀庆所钟，盖有所自云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1279831_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1182&endYear=1182')">1182年</a>　是年，有文送黄梦符。作品：《送黄梦符序》<div id='poem_1279787' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1279787' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1279787?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送黄梦符序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1182年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30187, "南宋", "王炎", "poem_title_1279787")'>王炎</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1279787_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1279787'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1279787'>予备员长沙郡文学，同舍聚而处者千指，而七闽黄梦符在焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1279787_comment'></div>未踰时即辞去，问其所向，将沿湘水过洞庭，下鄂渚，皆屈原、贾谊经行之地，使后人可以慨然增感者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1279787_comment'></div>谊由博士来为王傅，未为不得志也，然涉湘吊原，其辞气忧愤，无聊不平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1279787_comment'></div>及其赋鵩鸟，同死生，轻去就，太史公读其文，为之爽然自失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1279787_comment'></div>然有心于会理，则已与理为二；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1279787_comment'></div>用意于遣情，则已为情所滞矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1279787_comment'></div>吁，一穷固难忍哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1279787_comment'></div>梦符曩摄武冈教事，将翔矣，又跌而不升，千里倦游，顾安能无感？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1279787_comment'></div>然予闻柳子厚年少气锐，轩翥台省，而附离非人，遂摈外以没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1279787_comment'></div>韩退之应举则黜，立朝则斥，连蹇半生，暮年尹京兆，班从臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1279787_comment'></div>人生得丧荣悴悲喜相乘除耳，锐进则亟退，先抑则后伸，知道者所以不汲汲戚戚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1279787_comment'></div>梦符行矣，遇晴晖淑景，阴雨悲风，把酒哦诗，旅怀怏怏不自释，试补诵予说，当为予悠然一笑也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1279787_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1183&endYear=1183')">1183年</a>　在潭州教授任上，受到潭帅林栗器重。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1184&endYear=1184')">1184年</a>　与林栗唱和。作品：《和林宝文鹿鸣宴韵》《和林宝文喜雨》《和林宝文吹暑轩二绝》《再和林宝文三绝》《林宝文生日》<div id='poem_72462' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_72462' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/72462?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和林宝文鹿鸣宴韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1184年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a class='inlineComment2'>（王本作茎）</span>爽，天开火德昌。<div id='poem_sentence_6_72612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_72612'>慈皇年有永，大帝寿无疆。<div id='poem_sentence_9_72612'>乔枝方叠荫，瓜瓞寖垂芳。<div id='poem_sentence_9_72612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_72612'>储禁铜扉肃，官僚玉佩锵。<div id='poem_sentence_10_72612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_72612'>旌麾张十戟，笋簴列三厢。<div id='poem_sentence_11_72612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_72612'>恭命来南纪，驰情望左坊。<div id='poem_sentence_12_72612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_72612'>也叨持虎节，莫预献鸾觞。<div id='poem_sentence_13_72612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_72612'>海润涵群汇，霞骞映四方。<div id='poem_sentence_14_72612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_72612'>愿言申戬谷，夷夏仰元良。<div id='poem_sentence_15_72612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_72612'></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_72612_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1185&endYear=1185')">1185年9月</a>　九月，潭州教授任满，自长沙归乡，途径白石先妣茔所祭拜。作品：《九月到白石先妣茔所》<div id='poem_72330' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_72330' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/72330?labeling=true' target='_blank'>九月到白石先妣茔所<span class='inlineComment2'>（此以下自长沙归乡所作）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1185年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30187, "南宋", "王炎", "poem_title_72330")'>王炎</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_72330_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_72330'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_72330'>不瞻宰木过三年，霜露凄凉倍怆然。<div id='poem_sentence_0_72330_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_72330'>马鬣但惊荒宿草，龟趺未办表新阡。<div id='poem_sentence_1_72330_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_72330'>平生钟釜空遗恨，旧物杯棬半不传。<div id='poem_sentence_2_72330_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_72330'>鸿雁差池风雨急，吞声清泪彻黄泉。<div id='poem_sentence_3_72330_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1185&endYear=1185')">1185年</a>　在潭州有诗。作品：《除夜官舍独坐》《到城南园瞻南轩先生遗像》《用前韵荅彪讲书》《送李侍郎归衡州二首》《和谢安国求砚》《和谢安国韵》《送谢安国归清江》《题王倅来泉》《又题巢林》<div id='poem_72539' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_72539' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/72539?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除夜官舍独坐<span class='inlineComment2'>（此以下潭州所作）</span></a><span id='poem_sentence_1_72737_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_72737'>瞻望堂中人，玉色而山立。<div id='poem_sentence_2_72737_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_72737'>六学妙经纶，未试百之一。<div id='poem_sentence_3_72737_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_72737'>身存天下望，身没海内惜。<div id='poem_sentence_4_72737_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_72737'>此道付谁传，丹青但陈迹。<div id='poem_sentence_5_72737_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_72737'>楼边好山近，竹底凉风入。<div id='poem_sentence_6_72737_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_72737'>两鹤韵亦高，导我转湖侧。<div id='poem_sentence_7_72799'>稍添数髭白，不改两颊朱。<div id='poem_sentence_7_72799_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_72799'>松菊对主人，亦自清而腴。<div id='poem_sentence_8_72799_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_72799'>门外无车马，室中但<span class='inlineComment2'>（王本作有）</span>琴书。<div id='poem_sentence_3_72798'>南山有德人，一笑遗宠辱。<div id='poem_sentence_3_72798_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_72798'>岿然殿诸老，足以镇浮俗。<div id='poem_sentence_4_72798_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_72798'>一出上禁林，再出拥牙纛。<div id='poem_sentence_5_72798_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_72798'>本无圭组累，归去便野服。<div id='poem_sentence_6_72798_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_72798'>譬如山中云，润泽滋草木。<div "poem_title_72752")'>王炎</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_72752_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_72752'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_72752'>灵均葬鱼腹，贾傅问服臆。<div id='poem_sentence_0_72752_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_72752'>挽我来访古，穷鬼信有力。<div id='poem_sentence_1_72752_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_72752'>敢恨客毡寒，私喜无吏责。<div id='poem_sentence_2_72752_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_72752_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_72752'>今代谢叔源，人物居第一。<div id='poem_sentence_6_72752_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_72752_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_72752'>何以报明珠，更觉意羞涩。<div id='poem_sentence_9_72752_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_72753_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_72811' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_72811' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/72811?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送谢安国归清江</a><span class='authorDate'>（1185年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30187, "南宋", "王炎", "poem_title_72811")'>王炎</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_72811_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_72811'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_72811'>轩冕喜而忧，山林静而閒。<div id='poem_sentence_0_72811_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_72811'>宠辱皆妄事，请看槐梦安。<div id='poem_sentence_1_72811_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_72811'>世人悟此少，低头缚微官。<div id='poem_sentence_2_72811_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_72811'>足跌尚欲趋，翼倦不肯还。<div id='poem_sentence_3_72811_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_72811'>谢公湖海士，著眼高尘寰。<div id='poem_sentence_4_72811_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_72811'>心如玉壶冰，当暑气自寒。<div id='poem_sentence_5_72811_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_72811'>怀璧不愿市，懒上青云端。<div id='poem_sentence_6_72811_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_72811'>亲朋劝之仕，晚出弹其冠。<div id='poem_sentence_7_72811_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_72811'>未令据槐厅，亦合登蓬山。<div id='poem_sentence_8_72811_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_72811'>造物拙用大，束带来侯藩。<div id='poem_sentence_9_72811_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_72811'>掉头厌多事，袖手思故园。<div id='poem_sentence_10_72811_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_72811'>眉间已黄色，镜里犹朱颜。<div id='poem_sentence_11_72811_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_72811'>家住玉笥西，别有壶中天。<div id='poem_sentence_12_72811_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_72811'>千亩稻秫肥，三径松菊繁。<div id='poem_sentence_13_72811_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_72811'>妙得诗酒趣，小作杖屦缘。<div id='poem_sentence_14_72811_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_72811'>鸿飞霄汉外，蝉蜕尘埃间。<div id='poem_sentence_15_72811_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_72811'>我方自窘束，仰屋坐长叹。<div id='poem_sentence_16_72811_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_72811'>欲仕苦无津，欲归苦无田。<div id='poem_sentence_17_72811_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_72811'>野鹿念丰草，老骥困短辕。<div id='poem_sentence_18_72811_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_72811'>终当抱琴书，从公掩云关。<div id='poem_sentence_0_72853_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_72853'>荷花菱叶并篱落，平分十顷青玻璃。<div id='poem_sentence_1_72853_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_72918_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_72918'>揖湘妃，招月娣，御清风。<div id='poem_sentence_4_72918_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1185&endYear=1185')">1185年</a>　在潭州有词。作品：《念奴娇（海棠时过江潭）》<div id='poem_72931' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_72931' class='poemTitle id='poem_sentence_5_72931_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_72931'>莫道无情，嫣然一笑，也似曾相识。<div id='poem_sentence_6_72931_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_72931'>惜花无主，自怜身是行客。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_72931_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

href='/Writing/72917?labeling=true' target='_blank'>水调歌头<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>登石鼓合江亭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1185年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> -----title
临湘
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='2cf6ca2856084c159cfa29db3486a61b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2cf6ca2856084c159cfa29db3486a61b");'><span id='2cf6ca2856084c159cfa29db3486a61b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1189')">1187-1189年</a>，50-52岁</div><div id='2cf6ca2856084c159cfa29db3486a61b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年</a>　知临湘县。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年</a>　友人韩毅伯来访，月余相别，作序送之。作品：《送韩毅伯序》<div id='poem_1279790' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1279790' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1279790?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送韩毅伯序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1187年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30187, "南宋", "王炎", "poem_title_1279790")'>王炎</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1279790_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1279790'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1279790'>予昔屏居黟、歙间，韩毅伯自行在所西行过焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1279790_comment'></div>凡再至而再留，抵掌论事，意谓弃繻而出，乘传而归，富贵可以立致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1279790_comment'></div>予甚壮其志而羡其健决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1279790_comment'></div>厥后十有七年，予得邑临湘，毅伯游武昌，溯江而来，相见掀髯一笑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1279790_comment'></div>既而又历道别后崎岖艰苦之状，白发苍颜，相视而笑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1279790_comment'></div>予深悲其不遇而惜其志之不伸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1279790_comment'></div>留一月，将行，则曰：「予不复能返蜀矣，今将归老于淮山」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1279790_comment'></div>言毕，其意怆然不乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1279790_comment'></div>予解之曰：人生非鹿豕，岂能聚而不散？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1279790_comment'></div>离别不足恨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1279790_comment'></div>水涸，鱼处于陆，相呴以湿，相濡以沫，不如相忘于江湖，子庄子之语云耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1279790_comment'></div>关山间隔，相忘可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1279790_comment'></div>然毅伯与予一别十有七年，而后一见于此，又十有七年，则存亡未可知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1279790_comment'></div>于其行也，岂能无言？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1279790_comment'></div>凡物壮与老异，壮宜出，老宜复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1279790_comment'></div>木之归根，水之返壑，龙蛇之蛰，月之晦，雷之收声，皆是物也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1279790_comment'></div>毅伯壮年去家，足迹几半天下，今老矣，而不免于布衣，此命也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1279790_comment'></div>男子生以弧矢六射天地四方，示有志也，然穷通有命存焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1279790_comment'></div>其得志也举而措之事业，其不得志也卷而藏之环堵之中，故达则身泰，穷则心亨，在我何庸戚戚哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1279790_comment'></div>马文渊谓大丈夫穷当益坚，老当益壮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1279790_comment'></div>夫穷当益坚是矣，文渊之壮盖谓虽老而豪气不衰耳，其言未尽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1279790_comment'></div>士之少也用其壮于功名，老也用其壮于道义，文渊或未之知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1279790_comment'></div>昔林类鹿裘带索，拾穗而行歌，其言曰：「贫者士之常，死者生之终」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1279790_comment'></div>此能自宽者也，而未若颜歜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1279790_comment'></div>歜之言曰：「晚食可以当肉，安步可以当车」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1279790_comment'></div>此巧于处贫者也，而未若原宪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1279790_comment'></div>子贡相卫，结驷连骑，排藜藿，入穷阎，见原宪，宪摄敝衣冠见之，子贡曰：「先生岂病耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1279790_comment'></div>宪曰：「无财者谓之贫，学道而不能行者谓之病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1279790_comment'></div>若宪贫也，非病也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1279790_comment'></div>子贡闻其言，惭而去，悔之终身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1279790_comment'></div>宪之安于贫贱，盖闻道者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1279790_comment'></div>毅伯归乎哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1279790_comment'></div>淮水之滨，土厚泉甘，米贱而鱼肥，虽非故国，亦足以息肩弛担矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1279790_comment'></div>偃仰衡茅之下，啸咏东皋之上，回轩冕之眼，收功名之心，以求原宪之所乐，浮云富贵，亦于我何有哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1279790_comment'></div>夫玉在石，珠在泥涂，而其光彩见于山川，馀润及于草木。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1279790_comment'></div>士之所以不朽者，富贵不与也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1279790_comment'></div>达者或光耀于生前而寂寥于死后，穷者或枯槁于一时而芳馨于百世，彼此相较，其得孰多？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1279790_comment'></div>毅伯试归而图之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_37_1279790_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年</a>　期间，与友人韩毅伯唱和甚多。作品：《和韩毅伯知命》、、、《和韩毅伯拟别》《和韩毅伯求鹿皮韵》《次韵韩毅伯病疟》《次韵韩毅伯谢人惠茶》《和韩毅伯述怀》《次韵韩毅伯趣诸先辈送茶》《再用元韵因简县庠诸先辈》《江上为韩毅伯访得便舟》《再用元韵二首》《次韵韩毅伯拟别》《次韵韩毅伯别许宣教》<div id='poem_72212' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_72212' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/72212?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和韩毅伯知命</a><span class='authorDate'>（1187年）</span><span class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_72212_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_72212'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_72212'>春风盎盎杯中酒，流水潺潺膝上琴。<div id='poem_sentence_0_72212_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_72212'>个里有人真得趣，槐安一梦莫关<span class='inlineComment2'>（王本作可刳）</span>心。<div id='poem_sentence_1_72212_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_72212'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_72212_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_72480' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_72480' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/72480?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和韩毅伯拟别</a><span class='authorDate'>（1187年）</span><span id='poem_sentence_0_72480_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_72480'>不谓远游来此地，未能小隐待何时。<div id='poem_sentence_1_72480_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_72480'>惯看覆手仍翻手，休问开眉与皱眉。<div id='poem_sentence_2_72480_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_72480'>归去淮山访猿鹤，清风满袖自披披。<div class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_72754' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/72754?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和韩毅伯求鹿皮韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1187年）</span><span id='poem_sentence_0_72754_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_72754'>梅花肤革充靴材，人恰跣行畏伤足。<div id='poem_sentence_1_72754_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_72400'>示病维摩非实相，戏人疟鬼助文穷。<div id='poem_sentence_1_72400_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_72400'>笔头排闷诗千首，瓮面消愁酒一中<span class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_72709' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/72709?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵韩毅伯谢人惠茶</a><span class='authorDate'>（1187年）</span><span class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_72709_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_72709'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_72709'>一线金沙泉脉来，官焙初香春未雷。<div id='poem_sentence_0_72709_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_72709'>云龙小饼到天上，露芽濯濯千岩隈。<div id='poem_sentence_1_72709_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_72709'>缣缃空满石渠阁，鸿渐经成方有托。<div id='poem_sentence_2_72709_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_72709'>唤作酪奴真薄夫，雪乳云腴何可无。<div id='poem_sentence_3_72709_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_72709'>哦诗舌本费浇灌，畏遭水厄徒拘拘。<div id='poem_sentence_4_72709_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_72709'>岂知佩印乘轩客，醉饱犠尊羊鼎侧。<div id='poem_sentence_5_72709_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_72709'>要试江山第一泉，紫凤盘旋苍璧圆。<div id='poem_sentence_6_72709_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_72709'>书生品味惟三九，性自嗜茶如嗜酒。<div id='poem_sentence_7_72709_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_content_72482'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_72482'>洗盏从容对圣贤，笑谈未了意悽然。<div id='poem_sentence_0_72482_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_72482'>折腰我既惭陶令，肆志公宜学仲连。<div id='poem_sentence_1_72482_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_72482'>三沐三熏嗟已晚，一觞一咏乐馀年。<div class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_72710' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/72710?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵韩毅伯趣诸先辈送茶</a><span class='authorDate'>（1187年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30187, "南宋", "王炎", "poem_title_72710")'>王炎</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_72710_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_72710'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_72710'>脱腕符移日旁午，鱼眼浮香须一煮。<div id='poem_sentence_0_72710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_72710'>客来捧腹共轩渠，暂时拨置官文书。<div id='poem_sentence_1_72710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_72710'>喜客恨无鲜可击，满盂脱粟饥时吃。<div id='poem_sentence_2_72710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_72710'>睡魔不待巧挤排，雪花小啜清风来。<div id='poem_sentence_3_72710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_72710'>人生何苦浪驰逐，但得所求心自足。<div id='poem_sentence_4_72710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_72710'>意在春风晓露边，爱惜一旗轻万钱。<div id='poem_sentence_5_72710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_72710'>碾破云龙还不饮，滟滟金荷扶玉笋。<div "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>卯饭</span>动及午，姜糁菜丝烦自煮。<div id='poem_sentence_0_72684_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_72684'>异时甘脆屋渠渠，出自空肠千卷书。<div id='poem_sentence_3_72684'>泉新火活费裁排，呼奴更挈铜瓶来。<div id='poem_sentence_3_72684_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_72684'>蜀客见之心逐逐，暂借纸窗休茧足。<div id='poem_sentence_7_72684_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_72684'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_72684_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_72401' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_72401' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/72401?labeling=true' target='_blank'>江上为韩毅伯访得便舟</a><span class='authorDate'>（1187年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30187, "南宋", "王炎", "poem_title_72401")'>王炎</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_72401_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_72401'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_72401'>铜墨缠腰雪上头，人生一饱亦难谋。<div id='poem_sentence_0_72401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_72401'>天明忽暗酿梅雨，风暖又寒催麦秋。<div id='poem_sentence_1_72401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_72401'>老矣不堪时节换，粲然方幸故人留。<div id='poem_sentence_2_72401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_72401'>白云呼去淮山住，强为江边问买舟。<div id='poem_sentence_3_72401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_72401'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_72401_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_72377' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_72377' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/72377?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再用元韵二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1187年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30187, "南宋", "王炎", "poem_title_72377")'>王炎</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_72377_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_72377'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_72377'>牛千蹄角橘千头，叹息斯人善自谋。<div id='poem_sentence_0_72377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_72377'>文气如虹徒贯日，笔耕有谷不逢秋。<div id='poem_sentence_1_72377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_72377'>悠悠何啻十年别，得得才为一月留。<div id='poem_sentence_2_72377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_72377'>女嫁男婚吾未了，梦随鸥鹭学操舟。<div id='poem_sentence_3_72377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_72377'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_72377_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_72376' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_72376' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/72376?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1187年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_72376_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_72376'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_72376'>倦游莫忘大刀头，老去行藏要熟谋。<div id='poem_sentence_0_72376_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_72376'>少病若能如万福，上书安用学千秋。<div id='poem_sentence_1_72376_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_72376'>碧云合处来何缓，黄鹤飞时挽不留。<div id='poem_sentence_2_72376_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_72376'>后夜月明烟水阔，更呼儿辈洗瑶舟。<div id='poem_sentence_3_72376_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_72376'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_72376_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_72708' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_72708' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/72708?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵韩毅伯拟别</a><span class='authorDate'>（1187年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30187, "南宋", "王炎", "poem_title_72708")'>王炎</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_72708_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_72708'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_72708'>江头三老风樯急，诗叟欲行还却立。<div id='poem_sentence_0_72708_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_72708'>刚肠不解儿女悲，肯为别离襟袖湿。<div id='poem_sentence_1_72708_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_72708'>翰墨场中空白眉，宦游不遂休奔驰。<div id='poem_sentence_2_72708_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_72708'>平生讷室有秘诀，持以赠君君可归。<div id='poem_sentence_3_72708_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_72708'>静而无哗气方定，清而寡欲心自正。<div id='poem_sentence_4_72708_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_72708'>耳根毁誉等风波，眼界枯荣俱泡影。<div id='poem_sentence_5_72708_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_72708'>得此还家虽退藏，被褐怀玉中含光。<div id='poem_sentence_6_72708_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_72708'>踏破青鞋行万里，猛省昨非今近是。<div id='poem_sentence_7_72708_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_72708'>但看污渎有灵龟，莫道蹄涔无尺鲤。<div id='poem_sentence_8_72708_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_72708'></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_72708_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_72399' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_72399' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/72399?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵韩毅伯别许宣教</a><span class='authorDate'>（1187年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30187, "南宋", "王炎", "poem_title_72399")'>王炎</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_72399_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_72399'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_72399'>自说羁怀老更慵，淮山入梦碧丛丛。<div id='poem_sentence_0_72399_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_72399'>一尊醽醁人将别，三叠阳关曲易终。<div id='poem_sentence_1_72399_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_72399'>此去若无鸿雁信，相望<span class='inlineComment2'>（王本作忘）</span>未免马牛风。<div id='poem_sentence_2_72399_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_72399'>耕云钓月平生事，我亦谋归古歙中。<div id='poem_sentence_3_72399_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_72399'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_72399_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1188&endYear=1188')">1188年</a>　在知临湘任上，举荐临湘酒税官刘朋举。临别，写序相送。作品：《送刘监序》<div id='poem_1279791' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1279791' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1279791?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送刘监序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1188年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30187, "南宋", "王炎", "poem_title_1279791")'>王炎</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1279791_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1279791'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1279791'>上饶刘君朋举为临湘酒税官，与某同寮且二年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1279791_comment'></div>会靖之会同缺令，部使者直秘阁丁公行部至临湘，访邑吏贤否，某具言朋举廉谨习为吏，即檄摄会邑事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1279791_comment'></div>将行，余不得无言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1279791_comment'></div>靖之民与蛮猺杂居，议者往往谓非我族类，其心必异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1279791_comment'></div>然欲静而患扰，喜和而恶乖，尚廉而贱贪，其情与吾民同，非如虎豹蛟鳄不可扰驯者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1279791_comment'></div>汉永和中议增群蛮租税，尚书令虞诩持不可，曰：「异俗贪婪，难束以礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1279791_comment'></div>今猥增之，必有怨叛不从」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1279791_comment'></div>蛮果争贡布非旧约，遂叛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1279791_comment'></div>予闻今猺人衰困，边徼防托吏士不无侵渔，甚者掠其子女为臧获。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1279791_comment'></div>谚曰「禽困覆车」，此可戒不可玩也，固当抚之以静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1279791_comment'></div>先汉开凉州四郡，吏民相亲，酒礼之会上下通民，是以其俗风雨时节，谷籴常贱，少盗贼，有和气之应，贤于内郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1279791_comment'></div>余闻猺人与吾县吏相见，若结以恩信，至于脔肉行酒，与之饮啖，不立崖岸，则欢然相亲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1279791_comment'></div>否则悍然而怒，遂为怨雠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1279791_comment'></div>故当接之以和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1279791_comment'></div>昔孟尝为合浦太守，郡与交趾比境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1279791_comment'></div>前此守令采珠无节，珠徙交趾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1279791_comment'></div>尝到官未踰岁，去珠复还，百姓以为神明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1279791_comment'></div>今黄金丹砂皆猺人巢窟所产也，蛮猺之性本贪，为吏者毫发无求，则彼必敬慕，有求焉则以我为可易矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1279791_comment'></div>故当示之以廉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1279791_comment'></div>是三者之言非无验之言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1279791_comment'></div>夫富者赠人以财，而仁者赠人以言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1279791_comment'></div>余不敢言仁，然同寮之义又不敢无言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1279791_comment'></div>古今赠行之言众矣，大抵多颂而少规，而余于朋举有规而无颂，言之他人必以我为戆，言之朋举必以我为忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1279791_comment'></div>于是乎言。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1279791_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1189&endYear=1189')">1189年</a>　在知临湘任上，上书丞相留正。作品：《上留丞相》<div id='poem_1279554' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1279554' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1279554?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上留正丞相书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1189年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30187, "南宋", "王炎", "poem_title_1279554")'>王炎</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1279554_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1279554'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1279554'>炎窃谓人主天下之至尊，而民者天下之至卑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1279554_comment'></div>宰相之职于至尊者为近，而县令之职于至卑者为亲，故人臣之等级莫贵于宰相，莫贱于县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1279554_comment'></div>然民虽至卑，天下之根本也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1279554_comment'></div>朝廷之德意欲下达于斯民，则宰相始之，而县令终之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1279554_comment'></div>故自近岁以来，士之为县者若朝廷不遗其微贱，稍加擢用，非以今为可重，而以国之根本为不可轻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1279554_comment'></div>炎新安之下士也，其足迹固亦屡至于都门矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1279554_comment'></div>岁在己丑，始窃太常之第，陈丞相用事，不敢见焉，则以未尝试吏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1279554_comment'></div>岁在己亥，始获关升，赵丞相用事，不敢见焉，则以未脱选调也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1279554_comment'></div>岁在丙午，始脱选调，王丞相用事，不敢见焉，则以犹未试县也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1279554_comment'></div>今者承乏岳之临湘，终更而来，故敢有所谒于丞相之前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1279554_comment'></div>天下之事浅者不足言也，其深切者炎又不敢尽载于书，请试略言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1279554_comment'></div>相公论道经邦之暇傥赐观览，炎敢毕其区区之说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1279554_comment'></div>炎闻圣贤之论治必有本末源流，本源不差，末流自治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1279554_comment'></div>故孟子曰：「人不足与适也，政不足与閒也，惟大人为能格君心之非」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1279554_comment'></div>此端本澄源之论也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1279554_comment'></div>治之所出，心为本源；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1279554_comment'></div>心之所主，诚为本源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1279554_comment'></div>诚，天理也，不诚，人欲也，思诚者去人欲而返天理也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1279554_comment'></div>天理人欲存于方寸之地，一消一长，而庶事之有得失，人心之有从违，风俗之有厚薄，君子小人之有进退，中国夷狄之有屈伸，举系于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1279554_comment'></div>是故虚静恬淡，存其本心，以酬酢万微，经纬四海，此五帝三王之事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1279554_comment'></div>秉德徇道，致其忠诚，格君心之非，成天下之务，此伊、傅、周、召之事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1279554_comment'></div>士大夫有列于朝者众矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1279554_comment'></div>主德之有阙、治道之未善，谏官得以言之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1279554_comment'></div>赏罚之未公，贤鄙之未分，御史得以言之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1279554_comment'></div>而所以格非心者台谏不预焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1279554_comment'></div>盖台谏耳目之官也，故谏诤论辩，救人主之失于已形之后，迹显而功浅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1279554_comment'></div>宰相腹心之臣也，故辅赞弥缝，止人主之过于未形之先，迹微而功深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1279554_comment'></div>共惟相公笃实而不欺，清净而寡欲，刚方而有守，伟然为一时之大人，而天下之望归之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1279554_comment'></div>膺寿皇之眷顾，副主上之倚毗，则用力于治之本原，使无毫厘之差，以新盛德，以复大业，岂特相公以此自任，圣明固以是望之，朝野固以是期之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1279554_comment'></div>《诗》曰：「德輶如毛，民鲜克举之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1279554_comment'></div>我仪图之，惟仲山甫举之，爱莫助之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1279554_comment'></div>相公之视伊、傅、周、召，有其道，有其志，而又居其位，其于天下之重任不患其举而莫胜也，而爱莫助之之意，炎之私心盖拳拳焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1279554_comment'></div>惟相公恕其狂瞽，幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1279554_comment'></div>虽然，炎之来，为贫而仕之念未绝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1279554_comment'></div>昔者，虞廷用人之法，既纳其言，又明其功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1279554_comment'></div>孔门知人之法，既听其言，又观其行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1279554_comment'></div>四方之下吏辐凑于都城之内，而相公之言其可用者与其可弃者固亦不逃英鉴之明矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1279554_comment'></div>顾炎何为者，望虞舜之廷，升孔子之门，贵贱相远而实情未孚，不得无以藉手也，故为《湖北末议》八篇以自献其所言，为《临江刬弊》一编以自见其所行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1279554_comment'></div>而其意犹有不能自已者，故又以书先焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1279554_comment'></div>《诗》曰：「采葑采菲，无以下体」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1279554_comment'></div>古人不遗微贱，意盖如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1279554_comment'></div>惟相公矜其愚衷，幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1279554_comment'></div>干冒钧严，俯伏俟命，下情不胜战慄之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1279554_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1189&endYear=1189')">1189年</a>　在知临湘任上，丞相留正生日，有词贺之。作品：《水调歌头（留宰生日）》<div id='poem_72920' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_72920' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/72920?labeling=true' target='_blank'>水调歌头 留宰生日</a><span class='authorDate'>（1189年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30187, "南宋", "王炎", "poem_title_72920")'>王炎</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_72920_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_72920'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_72920'>爱日护轻暖，酝造小春时。<div id='poem_sentence_0_72920_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_72920'>桃溪云敛，一点郎星吐青辉。<div id='poem_sentence_1_72920_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_72920'>炼玉颜容难老，点漆精神如旧，不用摘霜髭。<div id='poem_sentence_2_72920_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_72920'>厌薄蓬莱景，戏踏两凫飞。<div id='poem_sentence_3_72920_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_72920'>潘花底，陶柳外，细民肥。<div id='poem_sentence_4_72920_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_72920'>万家喜色，融瑞气拥牙绯。<div id='poem_sentence_5_72920_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_72920'>凭仗春葱洗玉，领略朱樱度曲，引满又何辞。<div id='poem_sentence_6_72920_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_72920'>只待琴歌毕，安步上丹墀。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_72920_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1189&endYear=1189')">1189年</a>　在知临湘任上，有文。作品：《鱼鳞保甲编序》<div id='poem_1279799' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1279799' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1279799?labeling=true' target='_blank'>鱼鳞保甲编序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1189年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30187, "南宋", "王炎", "poem_title_1279799")'>王炎</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1279799_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1279799'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1279799'>止盗，令职也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1279799_comment'></div>警盗，尉职也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1279799_comment'></div>令不能止盗，故儆盗之事始切，而尉之责始重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1279799_comment'></div>临湘前此盗区也，其所以多盗有三：游手小民迁徙无定，一也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1279799_comment'></div>逋窜黥徒出没不常，二也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1279799_comment'></div>荡泊之人家于林薮，为盗窟穴，三也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1279799_comment'></div>乡俗间往往剽劫无虚月，吏士罢于奔命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1279799_comment'></div>前县尉三衢吕君谦始籍编户为鱼鳞保甲法，选其丁壮，联什伍，备器械，断贼蹊径，讥察之谨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1279799_comment'></div>其遇有警，鸣枹鼓，众即云集，盗皆缘手擒获无脱者，繇是临湘无盗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1279799_comment'></div>吕君去，保甲备坐随弛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1279799_comment'></div>阅三年，盗再发于境，巴陵簿赵君师移尉临湘，复修保甲法，视吕君所规画加详焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1279799_comment'></div>于是小民之游手者、黥徒之逋窜者俱无所容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1279799_comment'></div>盖赵君临事精悍，御下严明，往来田野毫发无侵于民，故有所施为，民乐趣之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1279799_comment'></div>是以盗贼屏迹，境内安堵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1279799_comment'></div>将具其事上之台府，某曰：「赵君勤其官能如是，尉之职举矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1279799_comment'></div>若夫教足以驯暴，政足以禁奸，固有任其责者，尉不与也」。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1279799_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1189&endYear=1189')">1189年</a>　在知临湘任上，为崇惠庙作记。作品：《岳州崇惠庙记》<div id='poem_1279836' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1279836' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1279836?labeling=true' target='_blank'>岳州崇惠庙记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1189年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30187, "南宋", "王炎", "poem_title_1279836")'>王炎</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1279836_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1279836'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1279836'>临湘东南三十里有山，石骨嶙峋，望之黝而苍，是谓古仙洞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1279836_comment'></div>广四寻，从五窍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1279836_comment'></div>度石穴，至内洞，必篝火挟服，仅可以入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1279836_comment'></div>洞后汇为池，以溉田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1279836_comment'></div>古仙名氏无传，洞旧有庙曰崇惠，秩在祀典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1279836_comment'></div>遇旱岁，祷岩下辄应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1279836_comment'></div>而庙之仆已久，方士刘知崇即山足为屋数楹，环山之人乐捐金帛，以助其成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1279836_comment'></div>既成，炎适至，求文记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1279836_comment'></div>炎按《祭法》，山川能出云物为风雨皆曰神，此山之灵盖法所当祭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1279836_comment'></div>炎因闵雨，三祷而三应，故能知而书其事，使邑人因祀事而敬之，复歌焉，以乐仙之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1279836_comment'></div>词曰：仙伯兮逍遥，共骑鹤兮云霄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1279836_comment'></div>西溺水兮东瀛洲，超然变化兮不可以留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1279836_comment'></div>农之田兮瘠田，仙珥节兮闵此民而勿去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1279836_comment'></div>白云横兮翠微，石室幽幽兮宜而燕娱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1279836_comment'></div>一窦之泉兮不溢不枯，仙顾而乐兮黄鹄翩其来归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1279836_comment'></div>有龙蛰兮于寒泉，潜而飞兮遥天仙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1279836_comment'></div>吹箫兮击鼓，老农酌醑兮互起舞，仙驭飞龙兮四郊甘雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1279836_comment'></div>旱不为灾兮年谷屡丰，我民敬恭兮，蒙仙之泽无穷。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1279836_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1279836'><span class='label'>按：</span>隆庆《岳州府志》卷九，天一阁藏明代地方志选刊本。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1279836_comment'></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

id='poem_sentence_12_72839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_72839'>忆昔初筮仕，吾母犹朱颜。<div id='poem_sentence_13_72839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' -----title
清江
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='ab7e099b253945c0ac1b521e247dc3d1_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ab7e099b253945c0ac1b521e247dc3d1");'><span id='ab7e099b253945c0ac1b521e247dc3d1_link'
