id='poem_sentence_18_72628_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_72628'>奈何复作远，揽袂还踌躇。<div id='poem_sentence_19_72628_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_72628'>公犹寄异邦，同是江南区。<div id='poem_sentence_20_72628_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_72628'>但虑怀与安，久客非良图。<div id='poem_sentence_21_72628_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_72628'>终当念坟墓，速归三径芜。<div id='poem_sentence_22_72628_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_72628'>昨言亦云然，岁寒勿盟渝。<div id='poem_sentence_23_72628_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_72628'></div><div id='poem_sentence_24_72628_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1192&endYear=1192')">1192年</a>　迁通判临江军，有词。作品：《蝶恋花（柳暗西湖春欲暮）》<div id='poem_72959' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_72959' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/72959?labeling=true' target='_blank'>蝶恋花<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（壬子）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30187, "南宋", "王炎", "poem_title_72959")'>王炎</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_72959_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_72959'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_72959'>柳暗西湖春欲暮。<div id='poem_sentence_0_72959_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_72959'>无数青丝，不系行人住。<div id='poem_sentence_1_72959_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_72959'>一点心情千万绪。<div id='poem_sentence_2_72959_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_72959'>落花寂寂风吹雨。<div id='poem_sentence_3_72959_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_72959'>唤起声中人独睡。<div id='poem_sentence_4_72959_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_72959'>千里明驼，不踏山间路。<div id='poem_sentence_5_72959_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_72959'>谩道遣愁除是醉。<div id='poem_sentence_6_72959_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_72959'>醉还易醒愁难去。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_72959_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1194')">1193-1194年</a>　在临江，权知军。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1195&endYear=1195')">1195年</a>　夏，在豫章会曾渐，作序送之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1195&endYear=1195')">1195年11月</a>　十一月，太上皇帝加尊号上表贺之。作品：《贺太上皇帝加上尊号表》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1195&endYear=1195')">1195年</a>　在临江为同年朱元成《清江集》作后序。作品：《清江集后序》<div id='poem_1279802' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1279802' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1279802?labeling=true' target='_blank'>清江集后序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1195年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30187, "南宋", "王炎", "poem_title_1279802")'>王炎</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1279802_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1279802'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1279802'>士生而有才，与有才而获用，用而获尽其所缊，皆天也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1279802_comment'></div>贾谊洛阳一少年耳，而论事汉庭，诸老先生尽出其下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1279802_comment'></div>今观「痛哭流涕」一书，终西京二百年，其文章议论未有及之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1279802_comment'></div>谊之才高矣，绛、灌辈非其比也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1279802_comment'></div>东京之末，士方驰骛于功名，而诸葛孔明、庞士元隐约襄汉之间，不轻以身从人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1279802_comment'></div>司马德操曰：「孔明卧龙，士元凤雏也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1279802_comment'></div>先主用之，俱以为军师，则其才有以先人，未有以相先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1279802_comment'></div>而谊之爵位不及绛、灌，士元之功业不及孔明，何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1279802_comment'></div>其才富，其年啬也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1279802_comment'></div>谊之死仅三十有三，士元三十有六耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1279802_comment'></div>然则生而有才，才而获用，用而不尽其缊，人欤，其天欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1279802_comment'></div>使谊不遽死，汉之制度礼文不应尽袭秦陋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1279802_comment'></div>士元尚存，则先主兼据荆益，可以北争中原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1279802_comment'></div>二君短命，非特其身之不幸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1279802_comment'></div>清江朱元成，某同年生也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1279802_comment'></div>其为人工属文，善论事，而年止四十，遂赍其志以没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1279802_comment'></div>某来丞郡，元成没已二十年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1279802_comment'></div>从其子达得君文一编，读之，笔力驱驰，意旨开阖，可以高视辈流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1279802_comment'></div>谢艮斋为序其文曰：「元成智足以决大疑，气足以任大事，势足以驰大名」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1279802_comment'></div>艮斋许与固甚严，而评论元成斯言不浮也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1279802_comment'></div>元成官爵不显于时，事业不著于天下，而徒见于文，如玉有白虹，珠有五色，虽掩于瓦砾，汩于泥沙，终不可夺其光彩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1279802_comment'></div>使天假以年，阅义理益精，更世故益多，而策天下事益熟，可以不朽者讵止于是哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1279802_comment'></div>方今人物眇然，士大夫劲特自立者盖少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1279802_comment'></div>故某读元成之文，叹息以悲，非特为一同年生之无禄也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1279802_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
鄱阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='5b66045b5bb54668bddbfb21ba2b6fae_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("5b66045b5bb54668bddbfb21ba2b6fae");'><span id='5b66045b5bb54668bddbfb21ba2b6fae_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1203&endYear=1204')">1203-1204年</a>，66-67岁</div><div id='5b66045b5bb54668bddbfb21ba2b6fae' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1203&endYear=1203')">1203年</a>　出知饶州，到任有谢表。作品：《饶州到任谢表》<div id='poem_1279482' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1279482' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1279482?labeling=true' target='_blank'>饶州到任谢表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1203年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30187, "南宋", "王炎", "poem_title_1279482")'>王炎</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1279482_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1279482'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1279482'>祝釐散史，甘弛担于田庐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1279482_comment'></div>起废误恩，滥把麾于邻郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1279482_comment'></div>荣似昼游之绣，惧增夕饮之冰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1279482_comment'></div>中谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1279482_comment'></div>伏念臣踽踽独行，栖栖平进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1279482_comment'></div>晚遇圣神之采择，遍更学馆之清华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1279482_comment'></div>兼摄郎曹，躐升戎监。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1279482_comment'></div>得踰其分，自速颠隮；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1279482_comment'></div>行负于言，徒深惩创。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1279482_comment'></div>方念过都之鹢退，敢期出塞之马归！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1279482_comment'></div>再阅期年，荐叨新命；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1279482_comment'></div>起之閒馆，畀以守符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1279482_comment'></div>虽徽、饶一水之相通，最为便地；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1279482_comment'></div>而颜、范二贤之所治，亦号名城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1279482_comment'></div>第旱涝之相仍，且公私之俱困。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1279482_comment'></div>欲施舍则财于何取，务趣办则民将不堪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1279482_comment'></div>驽缓无庸，鸿私难称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1279482_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下知人则哲，御众以宽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1279482_comment'></div>舍其旧而图新，俾之改过；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1279482_comment'></div>用所长而去短，试以拨烦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1279482_comment'></div>虽合弃捐，特加抆拭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1279482_comment'></div>臣敢不省躬玷阙，厉志廉平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1279482_comment'></div>因密迩于里居，易讲求于民瘼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1279482_comment'></div>广朝廷宽大之意，专务抚摩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1279482_comment'></div>消田里叹愁之情，稍苏凋瘵。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1279482_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1204&endYear=1204')">1204年</a>　未数月罢。作品：《登四望亭（饶州，甲子）》<div id='poem_72579' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_72579' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30187, "南宋", "王炎", "poem_title_72579")'>王炎</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_72579_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_72579'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_72579'>春老飞花尽，园林遍绿阴。<div id='poem_sentence_0_72579_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_72579'>凭高聊寓目，念远更伤心。<div id='poem_sentence_1_72579_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_72579'>剧郡才难称，衰年病易侵。<div id='poem_sentence_2_72579_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_72579'>不如休歇去，吾意决投簪。<div id='poem_sentence_3_72579_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_72579'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_72579_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
湖州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='e075ce47ab1f41bba62b19553f264cf1_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e075ce47ab1f41bba62b19553f264cf1");'><span id='e075ce47ab1f41bba62b19553f264cf1_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1207&endYear=1209')">1207-1209年</a>，70-72岁</div><div id='e075ce47ab1f41bba62b19553f264cf1' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1207&endYear=1207')">1207年12月13日</a>　十二月，以朝议大夫起知湖州。作品：《湖州到任谢表》<div id='poem_1279485' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1279485' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1279485?labeling=true' target='_blank'>湖州到任谢表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1207年12月13日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30187, "南宋", "王炎", "poem_title_1279485")'>王炎</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1279485_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1279485'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1279485'>便朝赐对，近辅班条，起诸閒散之馀，付以蕃宣之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1279485_comment'></div>喜非所望，惧不能堪<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1279485_comment'></div>伏念臣曩以散才，滥升清贯，老随灾至，命与志违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1279485_comment'></div>入三馆者四年，瑕疵不掩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1279485_comment'></div>把一麾者数月，疮痏已成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1279485_comment'></div>坐此罢归，宜其永废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1279485_comment'></div>乃从家食，骤得守符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1279485_comment'></div>况古称苕霅之间，湖山清远；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1279485_comment'></div>而今比京畿之内，事物浩穰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1279485_comment'></div>自揆何人，可居此地！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1279485_comment'></div>第缘疏贱，不敢控辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1279485_comment'></div>识暗虑疏，何以拨烦而治剧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1279485_comment'></div>年衰气惫，难于扶弱而仆强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1279485_comment'></div>纵欲佩韦，终虞伤锦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1279485_comment'></div>兹盖恭遇皇帝陛下皇明日照，圣度天函。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1279485_comment'></div>在知人而能官人，虽加遴选；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1279485_comment'></div>善救物而无弃物，亦或兼收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1279485_comment'></div>臣敢不益戒旷官，深思补过！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1279485_comment'></div>宁催科之政拙，惟务便民；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1279485_comment'></div>但宽大之意行，是为报国。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1279485_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1208&endYear=1208')">1208年12月</a>　乞守本官致仕。作品：《申省乞休致状》<div id='poem_1279532' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1279532' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1279532?labeling=true' target='_blank'>申楼同知状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1208年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30187, "南宋", "王炎", "poem_title_1279532")'>王炎</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1279532_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1279532'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1279532'>炎备员近郡，幸书一考，未以罪罢，皆赖万间帡幪之庇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1279532_comment'></div>自顾孤远，不敢数贡竿牍，若其感德慕谊，一饭不置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1279532_comment'></div>今有肺腑真情，不得不一干钧听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1279532_comment'></div>炎一介书生，少犹无用，况已衰迟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1279532_comment'></div>向者再负罪戾，家贫不能忘禄，不免一出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1279532_comment'></div>而湖州号称繁剧，本非炎之所堪，而又岁计阙乏，一切趣办，又非炎之所能，勉强在此，日忧旷败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1279532_comment'></div>且平生悔吝已多，今仰干造化之地，求解郡归老山林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1279532_comment'></div>盖炎进退狼狈，有不可不休致者三说，请试言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1279532_comment'></div>古语云「失之东隅，收之桑榆」，桑榆之收虽晚，尚或可救东隅之失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1279532_comment'></div>炎才疏智短，不能自卫其身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1279532_comment'></div>昔在东都以罪罢，继得郡楚东，又以罪罢，东隅之失多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1279532_comment'></div>今在此凛凛，恐不免百谪，及早收身，尚或可全晚节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1279532_comment'></div>此炎所以乞休致者一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1279532_comment'></div>又缘命薄数奇，晚岁多艰，昨在中都，连丧二子，及归山间，又丧荆妇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1279532_comment'></div>平生七男，六人夭折，今在者唯恕一子尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1279532_comment'></div>念其壮年初得一官，不欲留在身伴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1279532_comment'></div>恕秋间当赴官，迟迟不行，炎强之去也，于十月间到官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1279532_comment'></div>炎茕茕一身，独在官所，既无壮成子弟，又无可用臧获，饮食起居色色失节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1279532_comment'></div>夫以郡事之繁，日夕忧虑，而衣服饮食又自失节，更迟迟不去，未免丧生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1279532_comment'></div>每窃自怜，中夜感叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1279532_comment'></div>此炎所以求休致者二也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1279532_comment'></div>夫才德系朝廷重轻者，年至耆艾或不得谢事，盖国家之所倚赖，盖君父之所眷顾，资其谋猷，仗其忠力，则不可以翻然引去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1279532_comment'></div>如炎者一介散才，譬如九牛一毛，有之何益，无之何损？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1279532_comment'></div>兼以多难之馀，气衰胆薄，稍有忧虑，便觉头目昏瞆，心志怔悸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1279532_comment'></div>若更不求引去，郡事未免废弛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1279532_comment'></div>纵使为贫恋禄，岂可贪得不止？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1279532_comment'></div>此炎所以求休致者三也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1279532_comment'></div>炎旧因陈舍人英仲、刘郎中硕夫获登门墙，瞻拜不过一再。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1279532_comment'></div>及流落去国之后，亦不曾一贡记府之问，其迹若疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1279532_comment'></div>然蒙钧慈顾念，异于他人，所以肺腑有怀，辄敢罄竭言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1279532_comment'></div>炎又伏念若其不能揣分，有所希求，则不可以仰渎钧听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1279532_comment'></div>今欲归老山林，全晚节，保残喘，度相公必然矜念，是以言之不厌其详也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1279532_comment'></div>泽雉野麋，放之笼槛，纵之林薮，仁人君子不使一物不得其性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1279532_comment'></div>若蒙大造，获从所请，即未填沟壑之日，皆门下生死肉骨之恩也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1279532_comment'></div>冒犯威尊，下情震恐。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1279532_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1208&endYear=1208')">1208年</a>　在湖州有词咏怀。作品：《阮郎归（霅川作）》《小重山（至后一日长兴赵宰到郡并招归安乌程二宰及项广文同饭）》《临江仙（莫子章郎中买妾佐酒魏倅以词戏之因次韵）》《水调歌头（送魏倅）》<div id='poem_72929' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_72929' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/72929?labeling=true' target='_blank'>阮郎归 霅川作</a><span class='authorDate'>（1208年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30187, "南宋", "王炎", "poem_title_72929")'>王炎</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_72929_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_72929'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_72929'>几回幽梦绕家山。<div id='poem_sentence_0_72929_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_72929'>怯闻梅弄残。<div id='poem_sentence_1_72929_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_72929'>萧萧黄落客毡寒。<div id='poem_sentence_2_72929_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_72929'>不禁衣带宽。<div id='poem_sentence_3_72929_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_72929'>身外事，意阑珊。<div id='poem_sentence_4_72929_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_72929'>人间行路难。<div id='poem_sentence_5_72929_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_72929'>寻思百计不如闲。<div id='poem_sentence_6_72929_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_72929'>休贪朱两轓。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_72929_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_72912' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_72912' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/72912?labeling=true' target='_blank'>小重山 至后一日，长兴赵宰到郡，并招归安、乌程二宰及项广文同饭</a><span /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_72912_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_72912'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_72912'>日脚才添一线长。<div id='poem_sentence_0_72912_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_72912'>葭灰吹玉管，转新阳。<div id='poem_sentence_1_72912_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_72912_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_72912'>唤客对凝香。<div id='poem_sentence_4_72912_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_preface_72937_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_72937'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_72937'>试问休官林下去，何人得似高年。<div id='poem_sentence_0_72937_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_72937'>壶中不记岁时迁。<div id='poem_sentence_1_72937_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_content_72919'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_72919'>新涨鸭头绿，春满白蘋洲。<div id='poem_sentence_0_72919_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_72919'>小停画鹢，莫便折柳话离愁。<div id='poem_sentence_1_72919_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_72919'>飘缈觚棱在望，不用东风借便，一瞬到皇州。<div id='poem_sentence_2_72919_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_72919'>别酒十分酌，何惜覆瑶舟。<div id='poem_sentence_3_72919_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_72919'>从此去，上华顶，入清流。<div id='poem_sentence_4_72919_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_72919'>人门如许，自合唾手复公侯。<div id='poem_sentence_5_72919_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_72919'>老我而今衰谢，梦绕故园松菊，底事更迟留。<div id='poem_sentence_6_72919_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_72919'>早晚挂冠去，江上狎浮鸥。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_72919_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1209&endYear=1209')">1209年1月</a>　正月十五日，奏修堤岸，开辟新田，从之。<br /></div>

-----title
绍兴
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='fc9b49bbfc404047a2938d34a04ff465_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("fc9b49bbfc404047a2938d34a04ff465");'><span id='fc9b49bbfc404047a2938d34a04ff465_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1209&endYear=1209')">1209年</a>，72岁</div><div id='fc9b49bbfc404047a2938d34a04ff465' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1209&endYear=1209')">1209年1月24日</a>　二十四日放罢，罢任后，与子恕居绍兴府。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1209&endYear=1209')">1209年</a>　在绍兴有词咏怀。作品：《清平乐（越上作）》《清平乐》<div id='poem_72950' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_72950' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/72950?labeling=true' target='_blank'>清平乐<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>越上作</a><span class='authorDate'>（1209年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30187, "南宋", "王炎", "poem_title_72950")'>王炎</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_72950_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_72950'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_72950'>呢喃燕语。<div id='poem_sentence_0_72950_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_72950'>共诉春归去。<div id='poem_sentence_1_72950_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_72950'>春去从他留不住。<div id='poem_sentence_2_72950_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_72950'>落尽枝头红雨。<div id='poem_sentence_3_72950_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_72950'>老翁袖手优游。<div id='poem_sentence_4_72950_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_72950'>闲愁不到眉头。<div id='poem_sentence_5_72950_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_72950'>过了麦黄椹紫，归期只在新秋。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_72950_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
